###########################
# Annexation Events
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file
###########################

add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Removing temporary ideas
	id = annex.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.0"}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		remove_ideas = NoDoubleAnnexItalyEvent
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Flanders-Wallonia
	id = annex.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.1"}
	title = annex.1.t
	desc = annex.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.1.a
		add_political_power = 60
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = BEL
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = BEL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = WLL
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = WLL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = FLN
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FLN
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BEL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2"}
	title = annex.2.t
	desc = annex.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}

		SWI = {
			add_state_core = 760
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = FRA
					tag = NFA
					tag = FRP
					tag = OCC
					owns_state = 16
					owns_state = 21
				}
				owns_state = 943
			}
			SWI = {
				transfer_state = 943
			}
		}

		SWI = {
			clr_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			clr_country_flag = SWI_enemies_on_all_sides
			clr_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			clr_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance

			set_cosmetic_tag = SWI
		}

		puppet = SWI

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = FRA
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				SWI = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Take Romandie
		name = annex.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		trigger = {
			tag = FRA
			owns_state = 760
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					state = 760
				}
			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		SWI = {
			clr_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			clr_country_flag = SWI_enemies_on_all_sides
			clr_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			clr_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance

			set_cosmetic_tag = SWI
		}

		puppet = SWI

		SWI = {
			set_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BEL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SWI_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3"}
	title = annex.3.t
	desc = annex.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				}
				owns_state = 841
				841 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 841
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				owns_state = 841
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_state_claim = 841
			}
			add_state_core = 841
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				}
				owns_state = 106
				106 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 106
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				owns_state = 106
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_state_claim = 106
			}
			add_state_core = 106
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
			}
			add_state_core = 731
			add_state_claim = 769
			add_state_claim = 184
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ROM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RRM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				NOT = {
					state = 77
					state = 106
					state = 184
					state = 731
					state = 769
					state = 772
					state = 841
					state = 989
					state = 1076
				}
			}
			BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GRE
					GRE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					owns_state = 47 #Athens
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					OR = {
						state = 184
						state = 731
						state = 769
						state = 989
						state = 1076
					}
				}
				BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SER
					SER = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					owns_state = 107
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					OR = {
						state = 841
						state = 106
					}
				}
				BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROM
					is_in_faction_with = RRM
					ROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					RRM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					owns_state = 46
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					OR = {
						state = 77
						state = 772
					}
				}
				BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		puppet = BUL

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BUL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pact.110
				days = 1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pact.111
				days = 1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pact.112
				days = 1
			}
			} #transfering other parts of Bulgaria
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				}
				owns_state = 841
				841 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 841
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				owns_state = 841
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_state_claim = 841
			}
			add_state_core = 841
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				}
				owns_state = 106
				106 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 106
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				owns_state = 106
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_state_claim = 106
			}
			add_state_core = 106
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
			}
			add_state_core = 731
			add_state_claim = 769
			add_state_claim = 184
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ROM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RRM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Romanian liberation
	id = annex.6
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.6"}
	title = annex.6.t
	desc = annex.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 82
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 82
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 789
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 789
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 84
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 84
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 83
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 83
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 76
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 76
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 80
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 80
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 875
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 875
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ROM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = ROM
			}
			puppet = ROM
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 82
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 82
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 83
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 83
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 789
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 789
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 84
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 84
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 76
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 76
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 80
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 80
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 875
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 875
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				RRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = RRM
			}
			puppet = RRM

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = GER
						has_socialist_government = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = romania.103 # Form of Romanian government
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				RRM = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUL
			}
			transfer_state = 772
		}
	}

	option = { #Take Bessarabia
		name = annex.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = RUS
				tag = SOV
			}
			owns_state = 192
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 82
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 82
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 83
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 83
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 76
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 76
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 80
				}
				ROM = {
					add_state_core = 80
				}
			}

			RRM = {
				remove_state_core = 78
			}
			ROM = {
				remove_state_core = 78
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ROM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = ROM
			}
			puppet = ROM
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 82
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 82
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 83
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 83
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 76
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 76
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 80
				}
				RRM = {
					add_state_core = 80
				}
			}

			RRM = {
				remove_state_core = 78
			}
			ROM = {
				remove_state_core = 78
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				RRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = RRM
			}
			puppet = RRM

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					RRM = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = radical_socialist
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = radical_socialist
							popularity = 0.4
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					not_has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				country_event = romania.103 # Form of Romanian government
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate Romania without Hungarian states
		name = annex.6.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 789
			owns_state = 84
			owns_state = 82
			owns_state = 83
			owns_state = 76
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 789
				}
				ROM = {
					remove_state_core = 789
				}
				RRM = {
					remove_state_core = 789
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 84
				}
				ROM = {
					remove_state_core = 84
				}
				RRM = {
					remove_state_core = 84
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				ROM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = ROM
			}
			puppet = ROM
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 789
				}
				RRM = {
					remove_state_core = 789
				}
				ROM = {
					remove_state_core = 789
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 84
				}
				RRM = {
					remove_state_core = 84
				}
				ROM = {
					remove_state_core = 84
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				RRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				add_core_of = RRM
			}
			puppet = RRM

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					RRM = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = radical_socialist
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = radical_socialist
							popularity = 0.4
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {

		}

country_event = { #Serbian liberation
	id = annex.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.8"}
	title = annex.8.t
	desc = annex.8.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					state = 108
					state = 765
					state = 767
					state = 107
				}
				is_core_of = SER
			}
			SER = {
				remove_state_core = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 841
				NOT = {
					841 = {
						is_core_of = SER
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 48
						841 = {
							is_core_of = BUL
						}
					}
				}
			}
			SER = {
				add_state_core = 841
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 106
				NOT = {
					106 = {
						is_core_of = SER
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 48
						106 = {
							is_core_of = BUL
						}
					}
				}
			}
			SER = {
				add_state_core = 106
			}
		}


		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SER
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SER

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				SER = {

						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #CRO liberation
	id = annex.20
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.20"}
	title = annex.20.t
	desc = annex.20.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
			}
			CRO = {
				remove_state_core = 794
			}
		}

		CRO = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			remove_state_core = 104
			remove_state_core = 105
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CRO
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			CRO = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = CRO

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				CRO = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = CRO_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #The Irish Question

	id = annex.68
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.68"}
	title = annex.68.t
	desc = annex.68.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate

		name = annex.68.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = IRE
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			IRE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = IRE

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = GEX
				}
			}
			country_event = annex.69
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1940.03.29
				OR = {
					tag = POR
					tag = CAR
					tag = PAP
					tag = SPR
					AND = {
						tag = NFA
						is_in_faction_with = CAR
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = annex.184
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1940.03.29
				OR = {
					tag = POR
					tag = CAR
					tag = PAP
					tag = SPR
					AND = {
						tag = NFA
						is_in_faction_with = CAR
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = annex.186
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.68.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = IRE_CONQ

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Releasing Spain (if not POR)
	id = annex.73
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.73"}
	title = annex.73.t
	desc = annex.73.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

		trigger = {
			not_has_socialist_government = yes
		}

		name = annex.73.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}

		if = {

			limit = {
				country_exists = CAR
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SPR
						is_core_of = CAR
						is_core_of = CNT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = CAR } }
					add_core_of = CAR
				}
				CAR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				CAR = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		if = {

			limit = {
				CAR = {
					exists = no
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { SPR = { exists = no } }
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = SPR }
					remove_core_of = SPR
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = CAR } }
						add_core_of = CAR
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CNT = { exists = no } }
				every_state = {

country_event = { #National France accepts our offer!
	id = annex.104
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.104"}
	title = annex.104.t
	desc = annex.104.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = annex.104.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_subject_of = NFA
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = PREV
					is_core_of = FRA
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes
				}
				NFA = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = NFA
		add_stability = 0.1
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Arabia

	id = annex.106
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.106"}
	title = annex.106.t
	desc = annex.106.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #release a puppet Arabia
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = IRQ
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		name = annex.106.b
		log = "released puppet Arabia"

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = JBS
					is_core_of = SAU
					state = 754
					state = 679
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					AND = {
						state = 754
						OR = {
							ROOT = {
								tag = EGY
							}
							ROOT = {
								tag = JOR
							}
							ROOT = {
								tag = OTT
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 679
						OR = {
							ROOT = {
								tag = EGY
							}
							ROOT = {
								tag = JOR
							}
							ROOT = {
								tag = OTT
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 907
						ROOT = {
							tag = PER
						}
					}
					region = 28
				}
			}

			IRQ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = IRQ

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				IRQ = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to ally arabia
		trigger = {
			country_exists = IRQ
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = IRQ
				IRQ = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = annex.106.c
		log = "gave to ally Arabia"

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = JBS
					is_core_of = SAU
					state = 754
					state = 679
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					AND = {
						state = 754
						ROOT = {
							tag = EGY
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 679
						ROOT = {
							tag = EGY
						}
					}
					region = 28
				}
			}

			IRQ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.106.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						country_exists = IRQ
					}
					is_in_faction_with = IRQ
					IRQ = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		log = "chose to occupy"

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

		set_country_flag = SAU_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Libya

	id = annex.107
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.107"}
	title = annex.107.t
	desc = annex.107.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.107.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = OTT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_war_support = -0.03

		set_country_flag = LBA_CONQ
	}

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.107.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = OTT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = LBA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			"LBA" = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = LBA

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				"LBA" = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		"LBA" = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			clr_country_flag = LBA_idris_bacc
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = OTT
				}
				set_country_flag = LBA_idris_btfo
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = LBA_idris_btfo
			}
			set_country_flag = LBA_truepuppet
		}
	}

	option = { #Reintegrate them into the Empire (OTT only)

		name = annex.107.c
		trigger = {
			tag = OTT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		set_country_flag = LBA_CONQ
	}
}

		}

						ruling_party = radical_socialist

					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
				SUD = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate only Sudan

		name = annex.108.e

			factor = 25
		}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Persia

	id = annex.109
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.109"}
	title = annex.109.t
	desc = annex.109.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = OTT
				}
				add_state_claim = 413
				add_state_claim = 421
				add_state_claim = 417
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = SAU
						tag = JBS
					}
				}
				add_state_claim = 413
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.109.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

		set_country_flag = PER_CONQ
	}

	option = { #puppet

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_crush_persia
			}
		}

		name = annex.109.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = PER
					AND = {
						state = 352
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								owns_state = 291
								owns_state = 49
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28
					region = 129
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = PER

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				PER = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not_has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				PER = {
					remove_ideas = PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
					remove_ideas = PER_evolution_idea
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							not_has_elected_government = yes
						}
						PER = {
							remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									not_has_authoritarian_government = yes
								}
								PER = {
									remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = PER_REP
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #iran and kurdistan

		name = annex.109.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_crush_persia
				tag = OTT
			}
			any_owned_state = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = KUR
				KUR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = KUR
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			KUR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = KUR
					KUR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			puppet = KUR

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					KUR = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = radical_socialist
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = radical_socialist
							popularity = 0.4
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = PER
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28
					region = 129
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = PER

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				PER = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not_has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				PER = {
					remove_ideas = PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
					remove_ideas = PER_evolution_idea
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							not_has_elected_government = yes
						}
						PER = {
							remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									not_has_authoritarian_government = yes
								}
								PER = {
									remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = PER_REP
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = annex.111.t
	desc = annex.111.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.111.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

		set_country_flag = YEM_CONQ
	}

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.111.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = YEM
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			YEM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = YEM

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				YEM = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Siam

				tag = GER

		}

		# Saigon - 286 (VIE > CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = VIE

					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam

				remove_state_core = 286
			}
		}

			limit = {
				VIE = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = {
				remove_state_core = 286
			}
			VIE = {
				transfer_state = 286
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = {
				remove_state_core = 286
			}
			CAM = {
				transfer_state = 286
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

country_event = { #The fate of ceylon

	id = annex.119
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.119"}
	title = annex.119.t
	desc = annex.119.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}
		}

		name = annex.119.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = CEY
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CEY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		puppet = CEY

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				CEY = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupation

		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}
		}

		name = annex.118.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

		set_country_flag = CEY_CONQ
	}

	option = { #Integrate

		trigger = {

			OR = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}
		}

		name = annex.119.c

			factor = 80
		}

		add_political_power = -20
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = -0.02

		add_state_core = 422

		set_country_flag = CEY_CONQ
	}

	option = { #puppet

		trigger = {

			OR = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}
		}

		name = annex.119.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = CEY
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes

				transfer_state = PREV

country_event = { #Fate of Bolivia
	id = annex.135
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.135"}
	title = annex.135.t
	desc = annex.135.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.135.a #Liberate Bolivia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BOL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			BOL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BOL

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BOL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 872
				872 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				PRU = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				CHL = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 303
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				transfer_state = 872
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 872
				872 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				PRU = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			PRU = {
				transfer_state = 872
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = syndicalist
				}
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_1940_Elections
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_1940_Elections
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_PLP_Victory
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_PLP_Victory
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_MNR_Victory
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_MNR_Victory
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_Syndicalism_in_Bolivia
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_Syndicalism_in_Bolivia
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_PUR_Victory
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_PUR_Victory
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_populist
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_Disband_Parliament
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_Disband_Parliament
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				BOL = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = BOL_Rewrite_the_Constitution
					}
				}
			}
			BOL = {
				complete_national_focus = BOL_Rewrite_the_Constitution
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Occupy Bolivia
		name = annex.135.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = BOL_CONQ
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_war_support = -0.03
	}
}

	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MEX

			}

				transfer_state = PREV
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = MEE
					}

						#Trickery to remove Maria if they've already been puppeted as the empire

							ruling_party = social_liberal
							elections_allowed = no

							ruling_party = market_liberal
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = social_conservative
							elections_allowed = no
						}
						retire_country_leader = yes
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Pascual Ortiz Rubio"
							desc = "POLITICS_PASCUAL_RUBIO_DESC"
							picture = "Portrait_Mexico_Pascual_Rubio.tga"

							ideology = social_democrat_subtype
							traits = {}
						}

							name = "Juan Andreu Almazán"
							desc = "POLITICS_JUAN_ALMAZAN_DESC"
							picture = "Portrait_Mexico_Juan_Almazan.tga"

country_event = { #Fate of Galicia
	id = annex.146
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.146"}
	title = annex.146.t
	desc = annex.146.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.146.a #Liberate Galicia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 89
				owns_state = 73
			}

				add_state_core = 73
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROM
					tag = RRM
				}
			}
			GAL = {
				remove_state_core = 80
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = UKR
			}
			GAL = {
				remove_state_core = 80
				remove_state_core = 89
				remove_state_core = 91
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = RRM
					tag = ROM
					tag = UKR
				}
				owns_state = 89
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GAL
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				GAL = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = GAL
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes

						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}

			factor = 100
		}

			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = POL

					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 73
			}
			GAL = {
				add_state_core = 73
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 80
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROM
					ROM = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			ROM = {
				transfer_state = 80
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 80
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = RRM
					RRM = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			RRM = {
				transfer_state = 80
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {

						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		WLL = {
			clr_country_flag = BEL_SYN_REV
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Peacefull_Transition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = totalist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Revolution_By_Force
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Peacefull_Transition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists }
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Peacefull_Transition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_The_Government_Has_Failed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}

				complete_national_focus = WLL_The_Government_Has_Failed

		}

				has_government = authoritarian_democrat

				complete_national_focus = WLL_Hold_On_To_The_Monarchy
			}
		}

		name = annex.162.b

			factor = 10
		}

				country_exists = BEL
			}

		}

		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 827

			}

					tag = GER
					country_exists = GEA
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				owns_state = 827
			}
			every_owned_state = {

					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}

					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			puppet = VIE

				}

							ruling_party = radical_socialist
							elections_allowed = no
						}

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {

				owns_state = 670

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LAO
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				LAO = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			puppet = LAO

			if = {

					has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
				}
				hidden_effect = {

							ruling_party = radical_socialist

						}
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = radical_socialist
							popularity = 0.4
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 750

					owns_state = 826
				}
			}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = CAM
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}

	desc = annex.190.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

			factor = 100
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ANG
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ANG = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ANG

country_event = { #Fate of Somalia

	id = annex.192
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.192"}
	title = annex.192.t
	desc = annex.192.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #occupation

		name = annex.192.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SOM_CONQ

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}

	option = { #SOM

		name = annex.192.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 547
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {

				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOM
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}

				SOM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOM
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						state = 892 #Failsafe for Jubaland
					}
				}
				SOM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		puppet = SOM

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				SOM = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Liberia
	id = annex.210
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.210"}
	title = annex.210.t
	desc = annex.210.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LIB
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			"LIB" = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = LIB

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				LIB = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					"LIB" = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					}
				}
				"LIB" = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LIB
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			"LIB" = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = LIB

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LIB_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to JOR ally
		name = annex.239.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = JOR
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = JOR
				JOR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				819 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			JOR = {
				add_state_core = 819
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_core_of = JOR
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			JOR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to TUR/OTT ally
		name = annex.248.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {

					OR = {

						TUR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = OTT
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = OTT

							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {

				is_core_of = KUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ROOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = TUR
						}
						TUR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				TUR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
				else = {
					OTT = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to PER ally
		name = annex.248.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = PER
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = PER
				PER = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Occupy it

		}

			}

				}
			}
		}
		if = {

					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {

					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat

		name = annex.255.a

		}

			every_state = { #Coring
				limit = {

					is_core_of = CEN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}

					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			CEN = {
				clr_country_flag = CEN_centro_released

					load_focus_tree = Centroamerica_focus #Loads the Commie tree

						transfer_troops = no
					}

							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}

					annex_country = {
						target = GUA
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}

						NIC = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}

						target = NIC

				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GUA_CONQ
					country_exists = GUA
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HON_CONQ
					country_exists = HON
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ELS_CONQ
					country_exists = ELS
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NIC_CONQ
					country_exists = NIC
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = COS_CONQ
						COS = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					316 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 4
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -150
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_war_support = -0.15
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 3
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -120
			add_stability = -0.12
			add_war_support = -0.12
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 2
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.10
			add_war_support = -0.10
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 0
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else = { # Ought to never happen
			add_political_power = -10
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The giving of panama to central america
	id = annex.256
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.256"}
	title = annex.256.t
	desc = annex.256.d

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CEN_PAN_conq
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Give it all!
		name = annex.256.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PAN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			PREV = {
				add_core_of = CEN
			}
			CEN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the canal
		name = annex.256.b
		trigger = {
			685 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PAN
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					state = 685
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				add_core_of = CEN
			}
			CEN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep it annexed
		name = annex.256.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Eritrea
	id = annex.258
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.258"}
	title = annex.258.t
	desc = annex.258.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.258.a #Liberate Eritrea
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ERT
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ERT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ERT

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ERT = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.258.b #Give to Ethiopia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			ETH = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ERT
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ETH = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Occupy Eritrea
		name = annex.258.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = ERT_CONQ
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_war_support = -0.03
	}
}

		}

				add_state_core = 343 #Afyon

				add_state_core = 346 #Konya
				add_state_core = 49 #Ankara

			GUY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = GUY

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GUY = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.272.c #give it to CAF
		trigger = {
			CAF = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 300
		}


		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 687
					state = 1039
					state = 1078
					state = 1079
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			CAF = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Danish atlantic possessions Liberation
	id = annex.275
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.275"}
	title = annex.275.t
	desc = annex.275.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate ICE and keep Greenland (or don't do anything with them because you don't own them)
		name = annex.275.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = DEN
						is_in_faction_with = NOR
					}
					NOT = {
						tag = DEN
						tag = NOR
						tag = CAN
						tag = USA
						has_country_flag = swe_flag_sweden_norway
					}
					owns_state = 101
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ICE
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ICE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ICE

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ICE = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate ICE and give Greenland to DEN
		name = annex.275.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = NOR
					tag = CAN
					tag = USA
					has_country_flag = swe_flag_sweden_norway
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = DEN
					DEN = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = DEN
				}
				owns_state = 101
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ICE
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ICE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ICE

		DEN = {
			transfer_state = 101
			transfer_state = 926
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ICE = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate ICE and give Greenland to NOR
		name = annex.275.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = DEN
					tag = CAN
					tag = USA
					has_country_flag = swe_flag_sweden_norway
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = NOR
					NOR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = NOR
				}
				owns_state = 101
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ICE
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ICE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ICE

		NOR = {
			transfer_state = 101
			transfer_state = 926
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ICE = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate ICE and give Greenland to SWE-NOR
		name = annex.275.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = DEN
					tag = NOR
					tag = CAN
					tag = USA
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				SWE = {
					has_country_flag = swe_flag_sweden_norway
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = SWE
					SWE = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = SWE
				}
				owns_state = 101
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {

				is_owned_by = ROOT

			}

			transfer_state = 101
			transfer_state = 926

				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ICE = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist

					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = radical_socialist
						popularity = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

	}
